Select the number of minutes to play the sound(leave at 0 for unlimited play)\r\n2.  Slide the sleep timer to the on position to start the timer count down(Must have minutes added.).\r\n3.  Choose a sound by clicking on the image.  \"Name of Sound\" will be displayed across the image if it is curretnly active.\r\n4. To play multiple sounds, select the multi select option and click on the desired sounds to play.  Select the single select option and click on a non playing sound to go back to playing one wave at a time.\r\n6.  To save a selection make sure all desired sounds are playing and then click the save icon on the bottom right hand side and choose a save slot.  If there is already sounds saved in the slot it will light up green, they can be overwritten.\r\n7.  To load a selection click the disk icon and choose load and select what slot to load from.  I\r\n\r\nFor Xbox Users:\r\n1.  Left stick to move the mouse pointer\r\n2.  Right stick to scroll up and down on areas where you can.\r\n3.  'A' button selects sounds/items.\r\n4.
